																<div class="lexicon-label">Strong&#8217;s Definitions</div>
																<div class="lexStrongsDef"><p> <span class="strongsDagger"><a class="lexpop" rel="lexicon.strongsLegend">&#8224;</a></span><span class="Gk">οὐδείς</span> <span class="strgtrans">oude&#xED;s,</span> oo-dice&#39;; from <a title="Strong's G3761" href="/lexicon/G3761/kjv/tr/0-1/">G3761</a> and <a title="Strong's G1520" href="/lexicon/G1520/kjv/tr/0-1/">G1520</a>; not even one (man, woman or thing), i.e. none,
 nobody, nothing:&#8212;any (man), aught, man, neither any (thing), never
 (man), no (man), none (<span class="strongsPlus"><a class="lexpop" rel="lexicon.strongsLegend">+</a></span> of these things), not (any, at all, -thing),
 nought. 
</p></div>

														<div class="thayer-title no-print">
															<span class="og-header-toggle">STRONGS G3762:</span>
															<span>
																<span class="show-hide-ten"></span>
															</span>
														</div>
											    		<span class="lexicon-word"><span class="Gk">οὐδείς</span></span>, <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδεμία</span> (the feminine only in these passages: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/6/5/s_963005" id="si_1">Mark 6:5</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/4/26/s_977026" id="si_2">Luke 4:26</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/16/29/s_1013029" id="si_3">John 16:29</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/18/38/s_1015038" id="si_4">John 18:38</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/19/4/s_1016004" id="si_5">John 19:4</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/25/18/s_1043018" id="si_6">Acts 25:18</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/27/22/s_1045022" id="si_7">Acts 27:22</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/phl/4/15/s_1107015" id="si_8">Philippians 4:15</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/1/5/s_1160005" id="si_9">1 John 1:5</a>, and <span class="text-abbreviation">Rec.</span> in <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jas/3/12/s_1149012" id="si_10">James 3:12</a>), <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδέν</span> (and, according to a pronunciation not infrequent from <span class="author-abbreviation">Aristotle</span>, and <span class="author-abbreviation">Theophrastus</span> down, <span class="Gk maroon">οὐθείς</span>, <span class="Gk maroon">οὐθέν</span>: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/13/2/s_1075002" id="si_11">1 Corinthians 13:2</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">R<span class="lexsuper">st</span></span> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/19/27/s_1037027" id="si_12">Acts 19:27</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2co/11/8-9/s_1089008" id="si_13">2 Corinthians 11:8-9</a><span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/22/35/s_995035" id="si_14">Luke 22:35</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/23/14/s_996014" id="si_15">Luke 23:14</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/15/9/s_1033009" id="si_16">Acts 15:9</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span> text; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/26/26/s_1044026" id="si_17">Acts 26:26</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> brackets; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/13/3/s_1075003" id="si_18">1 Corinthians 13:3</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tdf.</span>; see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">μηδείς</span></span> at the beginning and <span class="author-abbreviation">Göttling</span> on <span class="author-abbreviation">Aristotle</span>, pol., p. 218; (<span class="author-abbreviation">Meisterhans</span>, Grammatik d. Attisch. Inschriften, § 20, 5; see Liddell and Scott, under the word <span class="Gk maroon">οὐθείς</span>; cf. Lob. Pathol. Elem. ii. 344); Alexander <span class="author-abbreviation">Buttmann</span> (1873) Ausf. Spr. § 10 Anm. 7) (from <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδέ</span> and <span class="Gk maroon">εἷς</span>) (fr. <span class="author-abbreviation">Homer</span> down), <span class="emphasis">and not one, no one, none, no</span>; it differs from <span class="Gk maroon">μηδείς</span> as <span class="Gk maroon">οὐ</span> does from <span class="Gk maroon">μή</span> (which see at the beginning); <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl2">1.</span> with nouns: masc, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/4/24/s_977024" id="si_19">Luke 4:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/16/13/s_989013" id="si_20">Luke 16:13</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/8/4/s_1070004" id="si_21">1 Corinthians 8:4</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδείς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἄλλος</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/15/24/s_1012024" id="si_22">John 15:24</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδεμία</span> in the passages given above; neuter, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/23/4/s_996004" id="si_23">Luke 23:4</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/10/41/s_1007041" id="si_24">John 10:41</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/17/21/s_1035021" id="si_25">Acts 17:21</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/23/9/s_1041009" id="si_26">Acts 23:9</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/28/5/s_1046005" id="si_27">Acts 28:5</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/8/1/s_1054001" id="si_28">Romans 8:1</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/14/14/s_1060014" id="si_29">Romans 14:14</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/gal/5/10/s_1096010" id="si_30">Galatians 5:10</a>, etc. <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl2">2.</span> absolutely: <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδείς</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/6/24/s_935024" id="si_31">Matthew 6:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/9/16/s_938016" id="si_32">Matthew 9:16</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/3/27/s_960027" id="si_33">Mark 3:27</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/5/4/s_962004" id="si_34">Mark 5:4</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/7/24/s_964024" id="si_35">Mark 7:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/1/61/s_974061" id="si_36">Luke 1:61</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/5/39/s_978039" id="si_37">Luke 5:39</a> (<span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span> in brackets); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/7/28/s_980028" id="si_38">Luke 7:28</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/1/18/s_998018" id="si_39">John 1:18</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/4/27/s_1001027" id="si_40">John 4:27</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/18/10/s_1036010" id="si_41">Acts 18:10</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/25/11/s_1043011" id="si_42">Acts 25:11</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/14/7/s_1060007" id="si_43">Romans 14:7</a>, and very often. with a partitive genitive: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/4/26/s_977026" id="si_44">Luke 4:26</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/14/24/s_987024" id="si_45">Luke 14:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/13/28/s_1010028" id="si_46">John 13:28</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/5/13/s_1023013" id="si_47">Acts 5:13</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/1/14/s_1063014" id="si_48">1 Corinthians 1:14</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/2/8/s_1064008" id="si_49">1 Corinthians 2:8</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1ti/6/16/s_1125016" id="si_50">1 Timothy 6:16</a>. <span class="Gk maroon">οὐδείς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">εἰ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">μή</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/19/17/s_948017" id="si_51">Matthew 19:17</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">Rec.</span>;
